| <span data-ttu-id="d2e68-444">進入</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d2e68-444">Entry</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="d2e68-445">值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d2e68-445">Value</span></span> |
